<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Shahba_mall1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Shahba_mall1.jpg/220px-Shahba_mall1.jpg" width="220" height="142" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Shahba_mall1.jpg/330px-Shahba_mall1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Shahba_mall1.jpg/440px-Shahba_mall1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="960" data-file-height="621" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Shahba_mall1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The <a href="/wiki/Shahba_Mall" title="Shahba Mall">Shahba Mall</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Aleppo boasts a vibrant <a href="/wiki/Nightlife" title="Nightlife">nightlife</a>. Several night-clubs, bars and cabarets that are open until dawn can be found throughout the city. Many bars are located in the old quarter of Jdeydeh quarter within ancient oriental mansions that provide special treats from the Aleppine flavour and cuisine along with local music.</p>
<p><i>The <a href="/wiki/Club_d%27Alep" title="Club d'Alep">Club d'Alep</a></i> opened in 1945, is a unique social club known for <a href="/wiki/Contract_bridge" title="Contract bridge">bridge games</a> and other nightlife activities. The <a href="/wiki/Aleppo_Public_Park" title="Aleppo Public Park">Aleppo Public Park</a> opened in 1949, is one of the largest planted parks in Syria, located near the Aziziyeh area, where the Queiq river breaks through the green park. <i>Blue Lagoon</i>, one of the favourite places of the Aleppine people, is the first water park in Syria. The <a href="/wiki/Shahba_Mall" title="Shahba Mall">Shahba Mall</a> of Aleppo is one of the largest shopping centres in the <a href="/wiki/Levant" title="Levant">Levant</a>. However, it was heavily damaged during the civil war and is currently abandoned.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aleppo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Aleppo_University,_Faculty_of_Arts_and_Humanities.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Aleppo_University%2C_Faculty_of_Arts_and_Humanities.jpg/220px-Aleppo_University%2C_Faculty_of_Arts_and_Humanities.jpg" width="220" height="117" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Aleppo_University%2C_Faculty_of_Arts_and_Humanities.jpg/330px-Aleppo_University%2C_Faculty_of_Arts_and_Humanities.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Aleppo_University%2C_Faculty_of_Arts_and_Humanities.jpg/440px-Aleppo_University%2C_Faculty_of_Arts_and_Humanities.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3645" data-file-height="1943" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Aleppo_University,_Faculty_of_Arts_and_Humanities.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The faculty of Arts and Humanities at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Aleppo" title="University of Aleppo">University of Aleppo</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>As the main economic centre of Syria, Aleppo has a large number of educational institutions. Along with the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Aleppo" title="University of Aleppo">University of Aleppo</a>, there are state colleges and private universities which attract large numbers of students from other regions of Syria and the Arab countries. The number of the students in Aleppo University is more than 60,000. The university has 18 faculties and 8 technical colleges in the city of Aleppo.</p>
<p>Currently, there are two private universities operating in the city: <a href="/wiki/Al-Shahba_University" title="Al-Shahba University">al-Shahba University</a> (SU) and <a href="/wiki/Mamoun_University_for_Science_and_Technology" title="Mamoun University for Science and Technology">Mamoun University for Science and Technology</a> (MUST).</p>
<p>Branches of the state conservatory and the fine arts school are also operating in the city.</p>
<p>Aleppo is home to several Christian and Armenian private schools as well as 2 international schools: <a href="/wiki/International_School_of_Aleppo" title="International School of Aleppo">International School of Aleppo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lyc%C3%A9e_Fran%C3%A7ais_d%27Alep" class="mw-redirect" title="Lycée Français d'Alep">Lycée Français d'Alep</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sport">Sport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aleppo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Sport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Aleppo_international.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Aleppo_international.jpg/220px-Aleppo_international.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Aleppo_international.jpg/330px-Aleppo_international.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/Aleppo_international.jpg/440px-Aleppo_international.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1200" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Aleppo_international.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Aleppo_International_Stadium" title="Aleppo International Stadium">Aleppo International Stadium</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The city of Aleppo is considered an important centre of <a href="/wiki/Team_sport" title="Team sport">team sports</a> with <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> being the most popular in the city. It is home to 5 major sport clubs, including <a href="/wiki/Al-Ittihad_SC_Aleppo" title="Al-Ittihad SC Aleppo">al-Ittihad SC</a>, <a href="/wiki/Al-Hurriya_SC" title="Al-Hurriya SC">al-Hurriya SC</a>, <a href="/wiki/Al-Yarmouk_SC_Aleppo" class="mw-redirect" title="Al-Yarmouk SC Aleppo">al-Yarmouk SC</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jalaa_SC" title="Jalaa SC">Jalaa SC</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ouroube_SC_Aleppo" class="mw-redirect" title="Ouroube SC Aleppo">Ouroube SC</a>.</p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">Basketball</a> is also very popular in the city. All of the 5 Aleppine major sport clubs participate in the men's and women's top division of the Syrian Basketball League.</p>
<p>Other popular sports being practiced by the major clubs in the city include <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Handball" title="Handball">handball</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volleyball" title="Volleyball">volleyball</a>, <a href="/wiki/Table_tennis" title="Table tennis">table tennis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Swimming_(sport)" title="Swimming (sport)">swimming</a>.</p>
<p>With a capacity of 53,200 seats, the <a href="/wiki/Aleppo_International_Stadium" title="Aleppo International Stadium">Aleppo International Stadium</a> is the largest sports venue in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup> Other major sport venues in the city include the <a href="/wiki/Al-Ittihad_Stadium" title="Al-Ittihad Stadium">al-Ittihad Stadium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Al-Hamadaniah_Stadium" title="Al-Hamadaniah Stadium">al-Hamadaniah Stadium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aleppo_7_April_Stadium" title="Aleppo 7 April Stadium">7 April Stadium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ri%27ayet_al-Shabab_Stadium" title="Ri'ayet al-Shabab Stadium">Ri'ayet al-Shabab Stadium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Al-Hamadaniah_Sports_Arena" title="Al-Hamadaniah Sports Arena">al-Hamadaniah Sports Arena</a>, <a href="/wiki/Al-Assad_Sports_Arena" title="Al-Assad Sports Arena">al-Assad Sports Arena</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bassel_al-Assad_Swimming_Complex" title="Bassel al-Assad Swimming Complex">Bassel al-Assad Swimming Complex</a>, <a href="/wiki/Al-Hamadaniah_Olympic_Swimming_and_Diving_Complex" title="Al-Hamadaniah Olympic Swimming and Diving Complex">al-Hamadaniah Olympic Swimming and Diving Complex</a> and <a href="/wiki/Al-Hamadaniah_Tennis_Complex" title="Al-Hamadaniah Tennis Complex">al-Hamadaniah Tennis Complex</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Municipality_and_international_relations">Municipality and international relations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aleppo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Municipality and international relations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The city of Aleppo is the capital of <a href="/wiki/Aleppo_Governorate" title="Aleppo Governorate">Aleppo Governorate</a> and the centre of <a href="/wiki/Mount_Simeon_District" title="Mount Simeon District">Mount Simeon District</a>. Aleppo City Council is the governing body of the city. The first municipality council was formed in 1868.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup> However, the governor who is being appointed by the president of the republic, has a supreme authority over the city and the entire governorate.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Subdivisions">Subdivisions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aleppo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Subdivisions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Districts in Aleppo could be sorted in 4 categories:</p>
<ul>
<li>Old quarters inside the walls of the ancient city.</li>
<li>Old quarters outside the walls of the ancient city.</li>
<li>Modern neighbourhoods.</li>
<li>Informal settlements.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Integrated_Urban_Development_in_Aleppo">Integrated Urban Development in Aleppo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aleppo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Integrated Urban Development in Aleppo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Covered_Suq_of_Aleppo2.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Covered_Suq_of_Aleppo2.JPG/220px-Covered_Suq_of_Aleppo2.JPG" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Covered_Suq_of_Aleppo2.JPG/330px-Covered_Suq_of_Aleppo2.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Covered_Suq_of_Aleppo2.JPG/440px-Covered_Suq_of_Aleppo2.JPG 2x" data-file-width="3264" data-file-height="2448" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Covered_Suq_of_Aleppo2.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<i>Souq al-Dira'</i>, maintaining its traditional role as a tailoring centre</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The "Integrated Urban Development in Aleppo" (UDP) is a joint programme between the German Development Cooperation (<a href="/wiki/GTZ" class="mw-redirect" title="GTZ">GTZ</a>) and the Municipality of Aleppo.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup> The programme promotes capacities for sustainable urban management and development at the national and municipal level.</p>
<p>The Programme has three fields of work:</p>
<ol>
<li>Aleppo City Development Strategy (CDS): promoting support structures for the municipality, including capacity building, networking, and developing municipal strength in the national development dialogue.</li>
<li>Informal Settlements (IS): includes strategy and management development of informal settlements.</li>
<li>The Project for the Rehabilitation of the Old City of Aleppo (OCA): includes further support to the rehabilitation of the Old City, as well as to a long-term oriented city development strategy.</li>
</ol>
<p>The UDP cooperates closely with other interventions in the sector, namely the EU-supported 'Municipal Administration Modernization' programme. It is planned to operate from 2007 to 2016.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preservation_of_the_ancient_city">Preservation of the ancient city</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aleppo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Preservation of the ancient city">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Khan_al-Wazir_with_Sahibiyah_mosque.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Khan_al-Wazir_with_Sahibiyah_mosque.jpg/220px-Khan_al-Wazir_with_Sahibiyah_mosque.jpg" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Khan_al-Wazir_with_Sahibiyah_mosque.jpg/330px-Khan_al-Wazir_with_Sahibiyah_mosque.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Khan_al-Wazir_with_Sahibiyah_mosque.jpg/440px-Khan_al-Wazir_with_Sahibiyah_mosque.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4288" data-file-height="2848" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Khan_al-Wazir_with_Sahibiyah_mosque.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Khan al-Wazir after rehabilitation</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Khandaq6_Alp.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Khandaq6_Alp.jpg/220px-Khandaq6_Alp.jpg" width="220" height="145" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Khandaq6_Alp.jpg/330px-Khandaq6_Alp.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Khandaq6_Alp.jpg/440px-Khandaq6_Alp.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2922" data-file-height="1923" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Khandaq6_Alp.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Al-Khandaq street, one of the restored streets of the old city</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>As an ancient trading centre, Aleppo's impressive <i><a href="/wiki/Souq" title="Souq">souqs</a></i>, <i>khans</i>, <i>hammams</i>, <i>madrasas</i>, mosques and churches are all in need of more care and preservation work. After <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, the city was significantly redesigned; in 1954 French architect <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9_Gutton" title="André Gutton">André Gutton</a> had a number of wide new roads cut through the city to allow easier passage for modern traffic. Between 1954 and 1983 many buildings in the old city were demolished to allow for the construction of modern apartment blocks, particularly in the northwestern areas (Bab al-Faraj and <a href="/wiki/Bab_al-Jinan" title="Bab al-Jinan">Bab al-Jinan</a>). As awareness for the need to preserve this unique cultural heritage increased, Gutton's master plan was finally abandoned in 1979 to be replaced with a new plan presented by the Swiss expert and <a href="/wiki/Urban_designer" class="mw-redirect" title="Urban designer">urban designer</a> <a href="/wiki/Stefano_Bianca" title="Stefano Bianca">Stefano Bianca</a>, which adopted the idea of "preserving the traditional architectural style of Ancient Aleppo" paving the way for <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">UNESCO</a> to declare the <a href="/wiki/Old_City_of_Aleppo" class="mw-redirect" title="Old City of Aleppo">Old City of Aleppo</a> as a World Heritage Site in 1986.<sup id="cite_ref-Aleppo_plan_99-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Aleppo_plan-99">[99]</a></sup></p>
<p>Several international institutions have joined efforts with local authorities and the Aleppo Archaeological Society, to rehabilitate the old city by accommodating contemporary life while preserving the old one. The governorate and the municipality are implementing serious programmes directed towards the enhancement of the ancient city and Jdeydeh quarter.</p>
<p>The German Technical Cooperation (<a href="/wiki/GTZ" class="mw-redirect" title="GTZ">GTZ</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Aga_Khan_Foundation" title="Aga Khan Foundation">Aga Khan Foundation</a> (within the frames of <a href="/wiki/Aga_Khan_Historic_Cities_Programme" title="Aga Khan Historic Cities Programme">Aga Khan Historic Cities Programme</a>) have a great contribution in the preservation process of the old city.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Twin_towns.2Fsister_cities">Twin towns/sister cities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aleppo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Twin towns/sister cities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_twin_towns_and_sister_cities_in_Syria" class="mw-redirect" title="List of twin towns and sister cities in Syria">List of twin towns and sister cities in Syria</a></div>
<p>Currently, Aleppo has 3 sister cities:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/France" title="France"><img alt="France" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Lyon" title="Lyon">Lyon</a>, France since 18 October 2000.<sup id="cite_ref-Lyon_151-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lyon-151">[151]</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey"><img alt="Turkey" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Flag_of_Turkey.svg/23px-Flag_of_Turkey.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Flag_of_Turkey.svg/35px-Flag_of_Turkey.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Flag_of_Turkey.svg/45px-Flag_of_Turkey.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="800" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Gaziantep" title="Gaziantep">Gaziantep</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> since 13 November 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus"><img alt="Belarus" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Flag_of_Belarus.svg/23px-Flag_of_Belarus.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Flag_of_Belarus.svg/35px-Flag_of_Belarus.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/Flag_of_Belarus.svg/46px-Flag_of_Belarus.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="450" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Brest,_Belarus" title="Brest, Belarus">Brest</a>, Belarus since 28 January 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_natives">Notable natives</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aleppo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Notable natives">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote">See also: <a href="/wiki/Rulers_of_Aleppo" class="mw-redirect" title="Rulers of Aleppo">Rulers of Aleppo</a></div>
<div class="div-col columns column-count column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2;">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abd_al-Rahman_al-Kawakibi" title="Abd al-Rahman al-Kawakibi">Abd al-Rahman al-Kawakibi</a>, thinker and religious reformer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abd_al-Rahman_Mowakket" title="Abd al-Rahman Mowakket">Abd al-Rahman Mowakket</a>, sculptor</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abed_Azrie" title="Abed Azrie">Abed Azrie</a>, composer and classical songs performer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ali_Sarmini" title="Ali Sarmini">Ali Sarmini</a>, painter</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amin_al-Hafiz" title="Amin al-Hafiz">Amin al-Hafiz</a>, former <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Syria" title="List of Presidents of Syria">president of Syria</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Antranig_Dzarugian" title="Antranig Dzarugian">Antranig Dzarugian</a>, Armenian novelist and poet</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Avraam_Russo" title="Avraam Russo">Avraam Russo</a>, Russian pop singer</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bassam_Kousa" title="Bassam Kousa">Bassam Kousa</a>, actor</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Buhturi" title="Buhturi">Buhturi</a>, Arab poet</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Charla_Baklayan_Faddoul" title="Charla Baklayan Faddoul">Charla Baklayan Faddoul</a>, reality TV figure</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Diana_al-Hadid" title="Diana al-Hadid">Diana al-Hadid</a>, sculptor</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fateh_Moudarres" title="Fateh Moudarres">Fateh Moudarres</a>, painter</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Francis_Marrash" title="Francis Marrash">Francis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Abdallah_Marrash" title="Abdallah Marrash">Abdallah</a> and <a href="/wiki/Maryana_Marrash" title="Maryana Marrash">Maryana Marrash</a>, writers and poets</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Acacius_Coussa" title="Gabriel Acacius Coussa">Gabriel Acacius Coussa</a>, cardinal and expert in canon law</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/George_Tutunjian" title="George Tutunjian">George Tutunjian</a>, <a href="/wiki/Armenian_revolutionary_songs" title="Armenian revolutionary songs">Armenian revolutionary songs</a> performer</li>
